***zip.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> zip (6082)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">zip</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">zips</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The high-pitched sound of a small object moving rapidly through air.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Energy; vigor; vim.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A zip fastener.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Zero; nothing.
<dl><dd><i>I know <b>zip</b> about economics.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A trip on a zipline.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A zip file.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">programming</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Synonym of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">convolution</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">type of mapping function</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An ounce of marijuana.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sound</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">whizz</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">zing</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">fastener</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">slide fastener</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">zip fastener</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">zipper</span> (<i>chiefly US</i>)</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">zip</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Zero; nothing.
<dl><dd><i>I know <b>zip</b> about economics.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<p><br />
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">zip</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>The high-pitched sound of a small object moving rapidly through air.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">whee</span>, whizz, zing</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">zip</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">zips</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">zipping</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">zipped</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To close with a zip fastener.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To close as if with a zip fastener.
<dl><dd><i><b>zip</b> one's lip</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To compress (one or more computer files) into a single and often smaller file, especially one in the ZIP format.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> programming</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To subject to the convolution mapping function.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>followed by a preposition</i>) To move rapidly (in a specified direction or to a specified place) with a high-pitched sound.
<dl><dd><i>The bullet <b>zipped</b> through the air.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (<i>followed by a preposition</i>) To move in haste (in a specified direction or to a specified place).
<dl><dd><i><b>Zip</b> down to the shops for some milk.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To make (something) move quickly
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> December 27,  Mike Henson,  “Norwich 0 - 2 Tottenham”, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport1/hi/football/16260392.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Tottenham also initially struggled to create genuine goal-scoring opportunities, with Bale, Luka Modric and Rafael van der Vaart <b>zipping</b> passes around to little effect.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To travel on a zipline.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> (11)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <a href="Translingual">Translingual section</a>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The Russian name for <b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></b> (<i>a</i>) is <b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></b> (<i>ā</i>), and in stressed syllables it has the sound of the long <b>a</b> in <i>f<b>a</b>ther</i>. In unstressed positions, it is pronounced as a schwa, like the <b>o</b> in <i>m<b>o</b>ther</i>. (Unstressed Russian <b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></b> (<i>a</i>) is pronounced the same as unstressed Russian <b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></b> (<i>o</i>).)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*a</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and, but</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*ō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁ōd</i> (presumed to be the ablative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*éy, h₁e</i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">õ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and, but</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Possible link with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">ar̃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">question particle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">a</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and, but</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">i</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">da</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and, but</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">ar̃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">if, whether</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">ir̃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">dár</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">still, yet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_8">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">a</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>but, and (introduces a new or different meaning).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теплый.html>тепло́</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вчера.html>вчера́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>хо́лодно</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sevódnja tepló, <b>a</b> včerá býlo xólodno.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It is warm today, <b>but</b> yesterday it was cold.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блоко</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:груша.html>гру́ша</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto ne jábloko, <b>a</b> grúša.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This is not an apple, <b>but</b> a pear.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>A</b> što?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Why so?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>a</b> to</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>or</b> else</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection_4">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle_3">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">a</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(colloquial particle used to seek confirmation) eh
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слышать.html>слы́шишь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty slýšišʹ menjá, <b>a</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Do you hear me, eh?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>придёшь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty pridjóšʹ sevódnja, <b>a</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">So are you coming today, then?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4_2">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ампе́р</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ampér</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5_2">Etymology 5</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">a</span>) (<i>invariable</i>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> he, she or it (used to point to a particular person)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:абажур.html>абажу́р</a> (9869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">abat-jour</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абажур.html>абажу́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">abažúr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абажур.html>абажу́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абажур.html>абажу́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абажур.html>абажу́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lampshade</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a visor, worn on the forehead to protect one's eyes from the sun</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> head</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> order, norm <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">pun on <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ажур.html>ажу́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ažúr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:абажур.html>абажу́ре</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsjó v <b>abažúre</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Everything's in order</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***аберрация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аберрация.html>аберра́ция</a> (23140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Aberration</i>, or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">aberration</i>. Both from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">aberrātiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аберрация.html>аберра́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aberrácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аберрация.html>аберра́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аберрация.html>аберра́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аберрация.html>аберра́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> aberration <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the distortion of an image from optical devices</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:симметричный.html>симметри́чная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:аберрация.html>аберра́ция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">simmetríčnaja <b>aberrácija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">symmetrical aberration</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:аберрация.html>аберра́ция</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>луча́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>aberrácija</b> lučá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">beam aberration</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:аберрация.html>аберра́ция</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>aberrácija</b> svéta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">aberration of light, light aberration</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> aberration <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">deviation from the norm or reality</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> aberration <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">change of position in the stars</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:абзац.html>абза́ц</a> (9380)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Absatz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абзац.html>абза́ц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">abzác</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абзац.html>абза́ца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абзац.html>абза́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абзац.html>абза́цев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> paragraph
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:абзац.html>абза́ц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">délatʹ <b>abzác</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a paragraph</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ть</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:начинать.html>начина́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вого</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:абзац.html>абза́ца</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">načátʹ/načinátʹ s (nóvovo) <b>abzáca</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to begin a (new) line/paragraph; to indent a line</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an indentation at the start of a paragraph.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:абзац.html>абза́ц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">délatʹ <b>abzác</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to indent</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">euphemism</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пизде́ц</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pizdéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">indentation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">о́тступ</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ótstup</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">абза́цный о́тступ</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">abzácnyj ótstup</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красный.html>кра́сная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:строка.html>строка́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krásnaja stroká</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">euphemism for пиздец</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пипе́ц</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pipéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писец.html>писе́ц</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">piséc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">капе́ц</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kapéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">абза́цный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">abzácnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:абзац.html>Абза́ц</a></b> translates as paragraph and is marked by an indentation and by the typographical character ¶. Conversely, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параграф.html>пара́граф</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parágraf</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> translates as section, is demarked by a section break, and by the symbol §. Compare also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздел.html>разде́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdél</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***абсорбция.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:абсорбция.html>абсо́рбция</a> (29483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">absorbēre</i>, present active infinitive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">absorbeō</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ab</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sorbeō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абсорбция.html>абсо́рбция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">absórbcija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абсорбция.html>абсо́рбции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абсорбция.html>абсо́рбции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абсорбция.html>абсо́рбций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>absorption</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>аб<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>су́рд<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>абсу́рднее.</i>

***абы.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:абы.html>абы</a> (25852)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">a</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абы.html>абы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aby</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>so that</li>
<li>if only
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i>Покорнейше <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просить.html>прошу́</a>, св. <a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:уведомить.html>уве́домить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайный.html>та́йно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:государь.html>Госуда́ря</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приключение.html>приключе́нии</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:абы.html>абы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взя́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дворец.html>дворе́ц</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надобно.html>на́добно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:империя.html>Импе́рии</a>.</i></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i>Pokornejše Vas prošú, sv. otéc, uvédomitʹ tájno samovo Gosudarja o mojóm priključénii, <b>aby</b> on menjá vzjal vo dvoréc, znáju, što nádobno bytʹ tepérʹ v Imperii.</i></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Obediently asking You, holy father, to let it know in secret the emperor himself about my journey, <b>if only</b> he would take me to the palace, I know, that it is necessary to be in the empire now. ― Aleksandr Arkhangelsky ‘Alexander I’, 2000 (cite taken from the National Corpora of Russian Language).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абы.html>абы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aby</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often in the negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> it doesn't matter <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">what/which/who/how</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яичко.html>яи́чко</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:абы.html>абы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сваренный.html>сва́ренное</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">S utra jemú jaíčko. Da ješčó ne <b>aby</b> kak svárennoje.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In the morning he has an egg. <b>It doesn't matter</b> how it's cooked.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отправить.html>отпра́вить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:письмо.html>письма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:санитарка.html>санита́рок</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:абы.html>абы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>каки́х</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердобольный.html>сердобо́льных</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:иначе.html>ина́че</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́йдет</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Otprávitʹ pisʹma móžno tólʹko čerez sanitárok, i ne <b>aby</b> kakíx, a serdobólʹnyx, inače ničevó ne výjdet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You can only send letters through the nurses, and <b>it doesn't matter</b> which ones but (they must be) compassionate, otherwise nothing will come of it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
